yaml-test-suite Framework Matrix - Test 4ABK

Spec Example 7.17. Flow Mapping Separate Values

YAML

{
unquoted : "separate",
http://foo.com,
omitted value:,
: omitted key,
}

Expected Events

+STR
+DOC
+MAP
=VAL :unquoted
=VAL "separate
=VAL :http://foo.com
=VAL :
=VAL :omitted value
=VAL :
=VAL :
=VAL :omitted key
-MAP
-DOC
-STR

Expected JSON

{
  "unquoted": "separate",
  "http://foo.com": "",
  "omitted value": "",
  "": "omitted key"
}
